***теребить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:теребить.html>тереби́ть</a> (11459)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">теребити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">terebiti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*terbiti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:теребить.html>тереби́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">terebítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to pull (at something), to finger, to play with, to pinch, to pluck (at)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to bother, to pester</li></ol>

***терем.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:терем.html>те́рем</a> (14804)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*termъ</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sh">trijem</i>/<i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh">тријем</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Polish" class="extiw" title="w:Old Polish">Old Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="zlw-opl">trzem</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:терем.html>те́рем</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">térem</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:терем.html>те́рема</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:терем.html>терема́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:терем.html>теремо́в</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">теремно́й</b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:теремок.html>теремо́к</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>tower, tower-room; a living area in a building or upper part of a building in the shape of a tower, especially in ancient Rus.</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>те́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:рема.html>ре́м</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:мужской.html>мужско́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 1c(1)  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
<a href = vnd.unilang:возможный.html>Возмо́жен</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>также</a> народно-поэтический <a href = vnd.unilang:вариант.html>вариа́нт</a> предложного <a href = vnd.unilang:падеж.html>падежа́</a>: <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:терем.html>терему́</a>.

***тереть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тереть.html>тере́ть</a> (7052)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*terti</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*terh₁-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to rub, rub by twisting, twist, turn</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">terō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to rub</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Greek_language" class="extiw" title="w:Greek language">Greek</a></span> <i class="Grek mention" lang="el">τρίβω</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="el-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">trívo</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to rub</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">trinti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to rub</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latvian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Latvian language">Latvian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lv">trīt</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to rub</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Armenian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Armenian language">Armenian</a></span> <i class="Armn mention" lang="hy">թրել</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="hy-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tʿrel</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to knead</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тереть.html>тере́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">terétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потереть.html>потере́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to rub</li>
<li>to polish</li>
<li>to rub sore, to chafe, to abrade</li>
<li>to grate, to grind</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тереть.html>тере́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">terétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тереться.html>тере́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">terétʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потереться.html>потере́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to rub oneself</li>
<li>to rub against smth
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кошка.html>ко́шка</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:тереться.html>тёрлась</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:об.html>об</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>мои́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>ноги</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kóška <b>tjórlasʹ</b> ob moí nogi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the cat was rubbing against my legs</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> deprecative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to hang around <i>(somewhere)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:тереться.html>тере́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:возле.html>во́зле</a> кого́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>terétʹsja</b> vózle kovó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to follow smb around</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:тереться.html>тере́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:среди.html>среди́</a> кого́-либо [[[МеждуRussian|[<a href = vnd.unilang:между.html>ме́жду</a>]] ке́м-либо]</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>terétʹsja</b> sredí kovó-libo [méždu kém-libo]</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to mix/mingle with smb; rub elbows/shoulders with smb</span></div></dd></dl></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:терзание.html>терза́ние</a> (25817)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:терзать.html>терза́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">terzátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ánije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:терзание.html>терза́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">terzánije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:терзание.html>терза́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:терзание.html>терза́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:терзание.html>терза́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>torment, agony, anguish <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">extreme pain</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>laceration, excruciation, stabbing</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:термин.html>те́рмин</a> (3680)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Via <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">termin</i> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Latin">Medieval Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">terminus</i>.

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:термин.html>те́рмин</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">términ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:термин.html>те́рмина</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:термин.html>те́рмины</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:термин.html>те́рминов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>term <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">word or phrase, especially one from a specialised area of knowledge</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:тереть.html>тёр</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ми.html>ми</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>но</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ло́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ги<span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>я</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 1-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 7a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-термин-</b>; интерфикс: <b>-о-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-лог-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>-и</a></b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-я</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***термический.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:термический.html>терми́ческий</a> (25105)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">therm(isch)</i> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ческий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-íčeskij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:термический.html>терми́ческий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">termíčeskij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">physics<span class="ib-comma">,</span> engineering</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> thermal, thermic</li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:терпеть.html>терпе́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">terpétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ли́вый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-lívyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:терпеть.html>терпе́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">terpétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***терпеть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:терпеть.html>терпе́ть</a> (1663)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">тьрпѣти</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tĭrpěti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*tьrpěti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:терпеть.html>терпе́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">terpétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потерпеть.html>потерпе́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to endure, to suffer, to tolerate, to stand
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наш.html>на́ша</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:команда.html>кома́нда</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:терпеть.html>те́рпит</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:поражение.html>пораже́ние</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Náša kománda <b>térpit</b> poražénije.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Our team is being defeated.</span></dd><dd>(literally, “<span class="e-literally">Our team <b>is suffering</b> a defeat.</span>”)</dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:терпеть.html>терпе́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>могу́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́того</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́ка</a>!</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Terpétʹ</b> ne mogú étovo čelovéka!</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I cannot <b>stand</b> that person!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to undergo (a change, <i>especially</i> a negative one)</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:тереть.html>тёр</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:петь.html>пе́ть</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 5c(4)X.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-терп-</b>; суффикс: <b>-е</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>. <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>

<h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>Значе́ние</a></span></h4>

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span>

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>мне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:терпеться.html>те́рпится</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:увидеть.html>уви́деть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:снова.html>сно́ва</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">mne ne <b>térpitsja</b> uvídetʹ jevó snóva</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I can't wait to see him again</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>вам</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:терпеться.html>те́рпится</a></b>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vam što, tak ne <b>térpitsja</b>?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">can't you wait any longer?; do you really have such an impelling urge?</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:терпеть.html>терпе́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">terpétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:терпеть.html>терпи́мый</a> (16064)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">терп(е́ть)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">terp(étʹ)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-кий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-kij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>astringent, tart, acerbic

***террор.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:террор.html>терро́р</a> (7872)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:террор.html>терро́р</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">terrór</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:террор.html>терро́ра</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:террор.html>терро́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:террор.html>терро́ров</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>terror (terrorist activities)</li></ol>
